msg:I made a special trip to Nanjing to see the Nanjing Museum's 90th anniversary special exhibition. The better hotels near Nanjing Museum are Zhongshan and Metropark. Later I discovered that these two buildings are also the tallest among a group of low buildings. Because I was very satisfied with the government hotels in Hunan and Hubei that I booked with Ctrip, I decided to choose Zhongshan after weighing this time. The Jiangsu Provincial Convention Center is also a government-backed hotel, and it is also the former site of the National Key Cultural Relics Inspirational Society. The environment of the hotel is very good. It is a garden-style hotel. The neighborhood is also very quiet. On the first night after I came out of Nampo, I was very glad that I did not stay at the Metropark. It was really noisy with the bustling traffic and people there, but it was really quiet at night here. many. From the hotel to the CAEXPO, you pass by the ruins of the Ming Palace. It‚Äôs a pleasant walk when the weather is good. It takes 10-20 minutes to walk. Along the way, you can see the rich colors of Nanjing, the yellow of sycamores and ginkgos, the red of maple leaves, and the Chinese Sophora japonica. The green is so beautiful. Before departure, I asked Ctrip customer service to help communicate with the hotel whether I could use the privileges to upgrade the room and provide complimentary breakfast, but they were rejected. Free is not necessary, so you can't be picky about the hotel in this regard. When I checked in, the front desk said that I could upgrade the room, but there were no vacancies at that time. There was only one ordinary standard room. After I was anxious to check in, I quickly went to Nanbo and checked in as booked. There was no upgrade. The sanitation and room service were both good. The room the hotel gave me was on a higher floor and I could see the Purple Mountain behind me. I was quite satisfied. The shortcoming of the hotel is that the sound insulation is not good. I couldn't sleep for two nights because of the noise from unknown rooms. On the first night, it was mainly women scolding each other, and men occasionally yelled a few times. The noise lasted until about 5 o'clock in the morning. The tragedy is that they continued to stay the second night. . . Also smashed things. . . I couldn't bear it anymore and called the front desk at 12 o'clock in the middle of the night. Please coordinate. The effect was not great and I stopped smashing things. However, the yelling didn't stop and I couldn't sleep until they went to bed at almost 2 o'clock in the morning. Later, the assistant lobby manager sent me a text message in the middle of the night saying that he could give me breakfast, thank you. The variety of breakfast was very rich, and I finally got some coffee. I only brought two bags of instant coffee, which was not enough for three days. I thought that there would be some in a hotel room of this level, but I still underestimated. Compared with the government hotels in Changsha and Wuhan, Zhongshan's service awareness still has room for improvement. I hope it can be improved. After all, the hardware of the room cannot be changed. Let's make up for it with service. With such good resources as Nanbo, I will definitely come back to the exhibition in the future. Even if the hotel has sufficient conference resources and does not care about individual tourists, if it does not make progress, it will only be reduced to a specialized conference hotel, which will waste such beneficial historical resources.
